select  s.specobjid, s.bestobjid, s.firstrelease, s.survey, s.sourcetype, s.class,  gal.ra, gal.raErr, gal.dec, gal.decErr, s.z, s.zErr,  gal.modelMag_g, gal.modelMag_r, gal.modelMag_i, gal.psfMag_g,  gal.petroMag_r, gal.petroR5#_r INTO mydb.LRG_CUT FROM Galaxy as gal   JOIN specobj as s on s.bestobjid = gal.objid WHERE (gal.flags & (dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)) ) > #    and ( gal.flags & (dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)) ) != dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    and ( gal.flags & (dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)) ) = #    and gal.petroMag_i > #    and (gal.petroMag_r > # or gal.petroR5#_r > #)    and (gal.petroMag_r > # and gal.g > # and gal.r > # and gal.i > #)    and ((gal.petroMag_r-gal.extinction_r < #)     and ((gal.petroMag_r - gal.extinction_r) < (# + (#/#) * (gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r) + # * (gal.dered_r - gal.dered_i) - # * #))     and ((gal.dered_r - gal.dered_i - (gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r)/# - #) < #)     and ((gal.dered_r - gal.dered_i - (gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r)/# - #) > #)     and ((gal.petroMag_r - gal.extinction_r + # * LOG1#(# * # * gal.petroR5#_r * gal.petroR5#_r)) < #))      or ((gal.petroMag_r - gal.extinction_r < #)     and ((gal.dered_r - gal.dered_i - (gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r)/# - #) > (# - (gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r)/#))     and ((gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r) > (# + # * (gal.dered_r - gal.dered_i)))     and ((gal.petroMag_r - gal.extinction_r + # * LOG1#(# * # * gal.petroR5#_r * gal.petroR5#_r)) < #))
SELECT TOP #   run, camCol, rerun, field, objID, ra, dec  FROM Galaxy  WHERE ((flags & (dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)   | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)   | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)) ) > #   and ( flags & (dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)   | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)   | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)) ) != dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)   and ( flags & (dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)   | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)) ) = #   and petroMag_i > #   and (petroMag_r > # or petroR5#_r > #)   and (petroMag_r > # and g > # and r > # and i > #)   and ( (petroMag_r-extinction_r) < #   and (petroMag_r - extinction_r < (# + (#/#) * (dered_g - dered_r) + # * (dered_r - dered_i) - # * #) )   and ( (dered_r - dered_i - (dered_g - dered_r)/# - #) < #)   and ( (dered_r - dered_i - (dered_g - dered_r)/# - #) > #)   and ( (petroMag_r - extinction_r + # * LOG1#(# * # * petroR5#_r * petroR5#_r)) < #) )   or ( (petroMag_r - extinction_r < #)   and ( (dered_r - dered_i - (dered_g - dered_r)/# - #) > (# - # *  (dered_g - dered_r)) )   and ( (dered_g - dered_r) > (# + # * (dered_r - dered_i)) ) )   and ( (petroMag_r - extinction_r + # * LOG1#(# * # * petroR5#_r * petroR5#_r) ) < # ) )
SELECT TOP #  s.plate,s.mjd,s.fiberid,s.z,s.zErr,s.zWarning,s.class,p.run,p.rerun,p.camCol,p.field,p.obj,cast(str(p.ra,#,#) as float) as ra,cast(str(p.[dec],#,#) as float) as dec,p.r,p.u,p.g,p.i,p.z  FROM ..SpecObj as s  JOIN ..Galaxy AS p ON s.bestObjID = p.objID  JOIN dbo.fGetNearbySpecObjEq(#,#,#) AS b ON b.SpecobjID = S.SpecobjID  WHERE s.zWarning = # AND (s.class = &&&)
SELECT G.ra,G.dec,G.type,G.CmodelMag_g,G.CmodelMag_r into mydb.CIRs FROM	Galaxy AS G    CROSS APPLY	dbo.fGetNearbyObjEq(@ra_#,@dec_#,#) AS GN   WHERE     (G.flags & dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)) = #  ORDER BY distance
select objects from both where the objIDs -- are the same. The output of the function is a table with the Galaxy Object -- ID and distance in arcmin from the input.  This query introduces the use of -- a JOIN to combine table contents.  Also, we use the &&& syntax, -- which will sort the output.  DECLARE @ra_# bigint set @ra_#=MYDB.CIRs(&&&) DECLARE @dec_# bigint set @dec_#=MYDB.CIRs(&&&)  --DECLARE @rad bigint set @rad=MYDB.CIRs(&&&)    SELECT G.ra,G.dec,G.type,G.CmodelMag_g,G.CmodelMag_r into mydb.CIRs FROM	Galaxy AS G    CROSS APPLY	dbo.fGetNearbyObjEq(@ra_#,@dec_#,#) AS GN -- this function outputs a table, so we have to do a join  WHERE     (G.flags & dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)) = # -- and the object is not saturated. f.PhotoFlags is a function that interprets the flag bits. ORDER BY distance 				-- sort these by distance
select  s.specobjid, s.bestobjid, s.firstrelease, s.survey, s.sourcetype, s.class,  gal.ra, gal.raErr, gal.dec, gal.decErr, s.z, s.zErr,  gal.modelMag_g, gal.modelMag_r, gal.modelMag_i, gal.psfMag_g,  gal.petroMag_r, gal.petroR5#_r INTO mydb.LRG_CUT FROM Galaxy as gal   JOIN specobj as s on s.bestobjid = gal.objid WHERE ((gal.flags & (dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)) ) > #    and ( gal.flags & (dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)) ) != dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    and ( gal.flags & (dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)    | dbo.fPhotoFlags(&&&)) ) = #    and gal.petroMag_i > #    and (gal.petroMag_r > # or gal.petroR5#_r > #)    and (gal.petroMag_r > # and gal.g > # and gal.r > # and gal.i > #)    and ((gal.petroMag_r-gal.extinction_r < #)      and (gal.petroMag_r - gal.extinction_r < (# + (#/#) * (gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r) + # * (gal.dered_r - gal.dered_i) - # * #))      and ((gal.dered_r - gal.dered_i - (gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r)/# - #) < #) and ( (gal.dered_r - gal.dered_i - (gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r)/# - #) > #)      and ((gal.petroMag_r - gal.extinction_r + # * LOG1#(# * # * gal.petroR5#_r * gal.petroR5#_r)) < #))      or ((gal.petroMag_r - gal.extinction_r < #)      and ((gal.dered_r - gal.dered_i - (gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r)/# - #) > (# - (gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r)/#))      and ((gal.dered_g - gal.dered_r) > (# + # * (gal.dered_r - gal.dered_i)))      and ((gal.petroMag_r - gal.extinction_r + # * LOG1#(# * # * gal.petroR5#_r * gal.petroR5#_r) ) < #))

SELECT TOP # fld.run, fld.avg_sky_muJy, fld.runarea AS area, ISNULL(fp.nfirstmatch,#)  FROM (   SELECT run, sum(primaryArea) AS runarea,  #e6*avg(power(cast(#. as float),#*sky_r)) as avg_sky_muJy  FROM Field  GROUP BY run  ) AS fld  LEFT OUTER JOIN (   SELECT p.run, count(*) AS nfirstmatch  FROM FIRST AS fm  INNER JOIN photoprimary as p  ON p.objid=fm.objid  GROUP BY p.run  ) AS fp  ON fld.run=fp.run  ORDER BY fld.run
